msg:The hotel is 8-10 minutes drive from the Lubei Civil Affairs Bureau, so I chose to stay at the InterContinental. Knowing that I was going to get the certificate, the hotel also made a simple arrangement. The check-in/out experience was very good.

Maybe the hotel is a bit old, and some parts of the room are aging and falling off, but the overall hygiene is OK.

The breakfast is hard to describe. The restaurant is decorated very old, the lighting is dim, the dishes are average, and not very appetizing. The chef and the staff chatted in front of the Western dishes, one at the counter and the other outside the counter, and neither wore a mask, which is not very good.

The location is very good, opposite the Tangshan Museum, and Wanda is a 3-minute walk away. There is also a snack street and a milk tea shop behind, which is very lively.

msg:After 5 years, I came to Tangshan again. Last time I was on a business trip, this time I took my children to experience this heroic city during the May Day holiday. Both times I chose to stay at the R&F InterContinental Hotel. The last time I stayed, I also made some comments and suggestions on the hotel's western restaurant. I can feel that the R&F InterContinental Hotel has always maintained the quality of the InterContinental brand. Although the hotel was full during the May Day holiday, the hotel was a little overwhelmed, and some services may have some flaws, but I saw that every staff member of the hotel was doing their best to strive to do their best and provide guests with the best possible quality services. Here I would like to pay tribute to every hard-working employee in the hotel! The hotel is in an excellent location, located in the center of Tangshan, opposite the Li Dazhao Principality and the Anti-Seismic Monument Square, and behind it is Wanda Plaza, eating, drinking and shopping at zero distance. It is about 3-5 kilometers away from the Tangshan Earthquake Site and Nanhu Park Scenic Area, which is very convenient. I will still choose the InterContinental Hotel next time.
